Kathāvatthuppakaraṇaṃ

Paṭhamo bhāgo

Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammā sambuddhassa.

Paṭhamo vaggo

1. 1.

Puggalakathā

1. Sakavādipucchā: puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti. -1.

Paravādipaṭiññā: āmantā.

Sakavādianuyogo: yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho-2. Tato so puggalo upalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti. -1.

Paravādipaṭikkhepo: nahevaṃ vattabbe.

Sakavādiniggaho: ājānāhi niggahaṃ.

----

1. Sacchikaṭṭhaparamaṭṭhenāti - syā
2. Sacchikaṭṭho paramaṭṭho - syā

[BJT Page 4] [\x 4/]

Anulomaṭhapanā: hañcī puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena,

Anulomapāpanā: tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho-1. Tato so puggalo
upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamattho'ti.
Anuloma āropanā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo
upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā.

Paṭilomaṭhapanā: no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo
upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.

Paṭilomapāpana: no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Paṭiloma āropanā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo
upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā.

Anuloma pañcakaṃ.

2. Paravādipucchā: puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti-2.

Sakavādipaṭiññā: āmantā. [PTS Page 002] [\q 2/]
Paravādianuyogo: yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti?
Sa. Paṭikkhepo: nahevaṃ vattabbe.
Paravādipaṭikammaṃ: ājānāhi paṭikammaṃ.

------

1. Saccikaṭṭho paramaṭṭho - syā
2. Sacchikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti - syā.

[BJT Page 6] [\x 6/]

Anulomaṭhapanā: hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena,
Anulomapāpanā: tena vata re vattabbe so saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo
nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Anuloma āropanā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: 'vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo
nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā.
Paṭilomaṭhapanā: no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo
nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Paṭiloma āropanā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā, no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo
nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā.

Paṭikammacatukkaṃ

3. Pa. Ni. Tvaṃ ce pana maññasi: vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo
nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti, tena tava tattha hetāya paṭiññāya hevaṃ
paṭijānantaṃ hevaṃ niggahetabbe atha taṃ niggaṇhāmi. Suniggahīto ca hosi.

Anu. ha: hañci puggelo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭha paramatthena,

Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalonūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.

[BJT Page 8] [\x 8/]

Anu. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no
ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā. [PTS Page 003] [\q 3/]

Paṭi. ha: no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti,
Paṭi. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.

Paṭi. Ā. Yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no
ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti idaṃ te micchā.

Niggaha catukkaṃ.

4. Pa. U: ese ce dunniggahite hevamevaṃ tattha dakkhā: vattabbe kho puggaloupalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo
upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti. No ca mayaṃ tayā tattha hetāya paṭiññāya hevaṃ
paṭijānattā hevaṃ niggahetabbaṃ. Atha maṃ niggaṇhāsi, dunniggahitā ca homa.

Anu. ha: hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena,

Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.

[BJT Page 10] [\x 10/]

Yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no ca
vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti
micchā.

Pari. ha: no ca pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.

Paṭi. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.

Paṭi. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no
ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti idaṃ te micchā.

Upanayanacakukkaṃ. [PTS Page 004] [\q 4/]

5. Pa. Niga: na hevaṃ niggahatabbe, tena hi yaṃ niggaṇhāsi.

Anu. ha: hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena,

Anu. Pā tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho, tato so puggalo upalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo
upalabbhati-1. Saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā.

Paṭi. ha: no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalouppalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.

Paṭi. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.

----
1. Nūpalabbhati-[P. T. S.]

[BJT Page 12] [\x 12/]

Paṭi. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no
ca vattabbe yo saccakaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo uppalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti idaṃ te micchā.

Nigamanaṃ: tena hi ye kate niggahe se niggahe dukkaṭe sukate paṭikimme. Sukata
paṭipādanā'ti

Nigamana-1. Catukkaṃ.

Paṭhamo niggaho.

Pa. Pu: puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti?
Sa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Pa. Anu: yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti?
Sa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe.
Pa. Ni: ājānāhi niggahaṃ.
Anu. ha hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena,
Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti. Anu. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalā nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no ca vattabbe yo [PTS Page 005] [\q 5/] saccikaṭṭho
paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā
Paṭi. ha: no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.

-----

1. Niggamana - sīmu. Machasaṃ.

[BJT Page 14] [\x 14/]

No ca vata re vattabbe puggalo nūpalababhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.

Paṭi. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no
ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti. Micchā.

Paccanika pañcakaṃ.

7. Sa. Pu: puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Sa. Paṭiññā āmantā.
Sa. Anu: yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe
Sa. Paṭikamma: ājānāhi paṭikammaṃ.
Anu. ha: hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena,
Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.

Anu. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no
ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micachā. Paṭi. ha: no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho
paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti,
Paṭi. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe pugagalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Paṭi. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no
ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā.
Paṭikammacatukkaṃ. [PTS Page 006] [\q 6/]
[BJT Page 16] [\x 16/]

8. Sa. Ni. Tvā ce pana maññasi: 'vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramatto tato so puggalo
upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti, tena tava tattha hetāya paṭiññāya hevaṃ
paṭijānantaṃ hevaṃ niggahetabbe, atha taṃ niggaṇhāmi. Suniggahito ca hosi.

Anu. ha: hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena,
. Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe 'yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.

Anu. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi 'vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no
ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā.

Paṭi. ha: no ce pana vattabbe 'yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggaloupalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Paṭi. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe 'puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.

Paṭi. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: 'vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no
ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti idaṃ te micchā.

Niggaha catukkaṃ.

9. Sa. U: ese ce dunniggahite hevamevaṃ tattha dakkha: vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tatoso puggalo
nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti. No ca mayaṃ tayā tattha hetāya paṭiññāya hevaṃ
paṭijānantā hevaṃ niggahetabbā. Atha maṃ niggaṇhāsi, dunniggahitā ca homa.

[BJT Page 18] [\x 18/]

Anu. ha: hañca puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena.
Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭha paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Anu. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati [PTS Page 007] [\q 7/]
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo
nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā.
Paṭi. ha: no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramatto tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Paṭi. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikatthaparamatthena, no
ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti idaṃ te micchā.

Upanayana catukkaṃ

10. Sa. Ni: na hevaṃ niggahetabbe, tena hi yaṃ niggaṇhāsi.
Anu. ha. Hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena,
Anu. Pā: tena vata re cattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Anu. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati scacikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no
ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā.

[BJT Page 20] [\x 20/]

Paṭi. ha: no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti
Paṭi. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo nūpalaba bhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Paṭi. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no
ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti idaṃ te micchā.
Nigamanaṃ: tena hi ye kate niggahe se niggahe dukkaṭe. Sukate paṭikamme. Sukatā
paṭipādanā'ti.

Nigamana catukkaṃ

Dutiyo niggaho. [PTS Page 008] [\q 8/]

11. Sa. Pu: puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa anu: sabbattha puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Pa. Avajānanā: na hevaṃ vattabbe.
Sa. Ni. Ājānāhi niggahaṃ
Anu. ha: hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena,
Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe 'sabbattha puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Anu. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: 'vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no
ca vattabbe sabbattha puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā.
Paṭi. ha: no ce pana vattabbe 'sabbattha puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.

[BJT Page 22] [\x 22/]

Paṭi. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Paṭi. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no
ca vattabbe sabbattha puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā -pe-

Tatiyo niggaho.

12. Sa. Pu. Puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: sabbadā puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Pa. Pavi: na havaṃ vattabbe.
Sa. Ni: ājānāhi niggahaṃ
Anu. ha: hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena,
Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe 'sabbadā puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Anu. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparatthena, no ca
vattabba sabbadā puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā.
Paṭi. ha: no ce pana vattabbe sabbadā puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Paṭi. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Paṭi. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena, no
ca vattabbe sabbadā [PTS Page 009] [\q 9/] puggalo upalabbhati
saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā -pe-

Catuttho niggaho.
[BJT Page 24] [\x 24/]

Sa. Pu: puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: sabbesu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe.
Sa. Ni: ājanāhi niggahaṃ.
Anu. ha: hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena,
Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe 'sabbesu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Anu. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca
vattabbe sabbosu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā.
Paṭi. ha: no ce pana vattabbe sabbosu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Paṭi. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe'puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Paṭi. Ā: yaṃ tattha vadesi: vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca
vattabbe sabbesu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti micchā. -Pe-

Pañcamo niggaho.

14. Pa. Pu: puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Sa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Pa. Anu sabbattha puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā'ti.
Sa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe.
Pa. Ni: ājānāhi niggahaṃ.
Anu. ha: hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena.

169. Sa. Pu: sveva manusso so devo'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Ā: manusso hutvā devo hoti, devo hutvā manusso hoti, manussabhuto añño, devo añño,
manussabhuto svāyaṃ svāyaṃ sandhāvatī'ti micchā -pe-
Sa. Ni: sace hi sandhāvati sveva puggalo ito cuto paraṃ lokaṃ anañño, hevaṃ-1. Maraṇaṃ na
hehīti. Pāṇātipāto'pi nūpalabbhati. Kammaṃ atthi, kammapivāko atthi, katānaṃ kammānaṃ
vipāko atthi, kusalākusale vipaccamāne svevāyaṃ sandhāvatīti micchā.

mahiso-2. Hotīti?

Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Saka. Ā. Manusso hutvā mahiso-2. Hoti, mahiso hutvā manusso hoti, manussabhuto añño,
mahiso añño, manussabhuto svevāyaṃ sandhāvatīti micchā -pe-
Sa. Niga: sace hi sandhāvati sveva puggalo ito cuto paraṃ lokaṃ anañño, hevaṃ maraṇaṃ na
hehīti. Pāṇātipāto'pi nūpalabbhati. Kammaṃ atthi, kammavipoko atthi, katānaṃ kammānaṃ
vipāko atthi, kusalākusale vipaccamāne svevāyaṃ sandhāvatīti micchā.

"Khandhesu bhijjamānesu
So ce bhijjati puggalo
Ucchedā bhavati diṭṭhi
Yā buddhena vivajjitā.
Khandhesu bhijjamānesu
No ce bhijjati puggalo,
Puggalo sassato hoti.
Nibbānena samasamo'ti.

Gati anuyogo.

87. Sa. Pu: parihāyati arahaṃ arahattā'ti.

Anabhāvakato āyatiṃ anuppādadhammo'ti.

Anabhāvakato āyatiṃ anuppāpadhammo, anu. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe 'parihāyati arahā
arahattā'ti.

88. Sa. Pu: parihāyati arahā arahattā'ti.

-Pe- thīnaṃ pahīnaṃ -pe- uddhaccaṃ pahīnaṃ -pe- ahirikaṃ
Pahīnaṃ -pe-anottappaṃ pahīnaṃ ucchinnamūlaṃ tālāvatthukataṃ anabhāvakataṃ āyatiṃ
anuppādadhammanti. Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.

Anu. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe 'parihāyati arahā arahattā'ti.

abbuḷhesiko niraggalo ariyo pannaddhajo pannabhāro visaññutto suvijitavijayo. Dukkhaṃ

Arahā arahattā'ti.

Oghapāso samuhato" ti.
Attheva suttanto'ti.

Sa. Niga: tena hi na vattabbaṃ 'atthi chinnassa chediyanti. '

3. Duguṇaṃ - pu.

Selo yathā ekaghano
Vātena na samīrati, evaṃ rūpā rasā saddā
Gandhā phassā ca kevalā

Iṭṭhā dhammā aniṭṭhā ca
Nappavedhanti tādino,
hitaṃ cittaṃ vippamuttaṃ
Vayaṃ cassā'nu passatī" ti. [A.]

Attheva suttanto'ti.

saṅgaṇikārāmātā yathā vimuttaṃ cittaṃ na paccavekkhati. Ime kho bhikkave, pañca dhammā
Samayavimuttassa bhikkhuno parihānāya saṃvattantīti" [b.] Attheva suttanto'ti. Sa. Paṭiññā:
āmantā.
Pa. Niga: tena hi paribhāyati arahā arahattā'ti.

1. 3.
Brahmacariyakathā

1. Sa. Pu: natthi devesu brahmacariyavāso'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
[PTS Page 094] [\q 94/]
Sa. Anu: sabbe devā jaḷā phalamugā aviñgñū hatthasaṃvācikā na paṭibalā
subhāsitadubbhāsitānaṃ atthamaññātuṃ, sabbe devā na buddhe pasannā na dhamme
pasannā na saṅghe pasannā, na
Buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ payirupāsanti, na buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ pañhaṃ
Pucchanti, na buddhena bhagavatā pañhe vissajjite attamanā,
Sabbe devā kammāvaraṇena samannāgatā kilesāvaraṇena samannāgatā vipākāvaraṇena
samannāgatā assaddhā acachandikā
Duppaññā abhabbā niyāmaṃ okkamituṃ kusalesu dhammesu
Sammattaṃ, sabbe devā mātughātakā pītughātakā arahantaghātakā ruhiruppādakā
saṅghabhedakā, sabbe devā
Pāṇātipātino adinnādāyino kāmesu micchācārino
Musāvādito pisunāvācā pharusāvācā samphappalāpino
Abhijjhāluno byāpannacittā micchādiṭṭhikā'ti.

Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

[BJT Page 254] [\x 254/]

Sa. Anu: nanu atthi devā ajaḷā anelamugā viññū na hatthasaṃvācikā
Paṭibalā subhāsitadubbhāsitānaṃ atthamaññātaṃ, atthi devā buddhe pasannā dhamme
pasannā saṅghe pasannā, buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ payirupāsānti, buddhaṃbhagavantaṃ
pañhaṃ pucchanti,
Buddhena bhagavatā pañhe vissajjite attamanā honti, atthi
Devā na kammācaraṇena samannāgatā, na kilesācaraṇena
Samannāgatā, na vipākācaraṇena samannāgatā, saddhāchandikā
Paññāvanto bhabbā niyāmaṃ dhammaṃ okkamituṃ kusalesu
Dhammesu sammattaṃ, atthi devā na mātughātakā na pītughātakā na arahantaghātakā na
ruhiruppādakā na saṅghabhedakā. Atthi
Devā na pāṇātipātino na adinnādāyino na kāmesu
Micchācārino na musāvādino na pisunāvācā na
Pharusāvācā na samphappalāpino na abhijjhāluno na avyāpannacittā sammādiṭṭhikā'ti.

Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Anu. ha: hañci atthi devā ajaḷā anelamugā viñgñū na hatthasaṃvācikā
[PTS Page 095] [\q 95/]
Paṭibalā subhāsitadubbhāsitānaṃ atthamaññātuṃ -pe- atthi devā
Buddhe pasannā -pe- sammādiṭṭhikā,
Anu. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe "natthi devesu brahmacariyavāso"ti.
2. Pa. Pu: atthi devesu brahmacariyavāso'ti.
Sa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Pa. Anu: atthi tattha pabbajjā muṇḍiyaṃ kāsāvadhāraṇā pattadhāraṇā.
Devesu sammāsambuddhā uppajjanti, paccekasambuddhā
Uppajjanti, sāvakayugaṃ uppajjatī'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

3. Sa. Pu: devesu pabbajjā natthi'ti natthi devesu brahmacariyavāso'ti.

[BJT Page 256] [\x 256/]

Sa. Anu: yattha atthi pabbajjā tattheva brahmacariyavāso, yattha natthi
Pabbajjā natthi tattha brahmacariyavāso'ti.

Sa. Anu: yattha atthi pabbajjā tattheva brahmacariyavāso, yattha natthi
Pabbajjā natthi tattha brahmacariyavāso'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: yo pabbajati-1. Tasseva brahmacariyavāso, yo na pabbajati
Natthi tassa brahmacariyavāso'ti. Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

natthi

Muṇḍiyaṃ natthi tattha brahmacariyavāso'ti.

Sa. Anu: yo muṇḍo hoti tasse'va brahmacariyavāso, yo muṇḍo na hoti natthi tassa
brahmacariyavāse'ti.
[PTS Page 096] [\q 96/]
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

14. Pa. Pu: atthi manusse brahmacariyavāso'ti.
Sa. Vi: atthi yattha atthi, atthi yattha natthi'ti.
Pa. Anu: paccantimesu janapadesu atthī yattha atthī, atthī yattha natthī
Brahmacariyavāso, miḷakkhesu aviññatāresu yattha natthi gati bhikkhūnaṃ bhīkhkhunīnaṃ
upāsakānaṃ upāsikānaṃ, majjhimesu janapadesu atthī yattha atthī, atthī yattha natthi
brahmacariyavāso'ti. Sa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

15. Pa. Pu: manusse atthi yattha atthi, atthi yattha natthi brahmacariyavāso'ti. Sa. Paṭiññā:
āmantā. Pa. Pu: kattha atthi, kattha natthi'ti.
Sa. Vi: paccantimesu janapadesu natthi brahmacariyavāso miḷakkhesu
Aviññātāresu yattha natthi gati bhikkhūnaṃ bhikkhunīnaṃ upāsakānaṃ
Upāsikānaṃ majjhimesu janapadesu atthi brahmacariyavāso'ti.
Pa. Anu: paccantimesu janapadesu natthi brahmacariyavāso miḷakkhesu

Upāsikānanti.
Sa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Pa. Pu: majjhimesu janapadesu natthi brahmacariyavāso'ti.

17. Pa. Pu: atthi devesu brahmacariyavāso'ti.

Uttarakuruke ca manusse adhigaṇhanti deve ca tāvatiṃ se. Katamehi tīhi? Sūrā, satimanto,
idha brahmacariyavāso'ti. [A.]

[PTS Page 100] [\q 100/]

Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-
18. Sa. Pu: anāgāmissa puggalassa pañcorambhāgiyāni saṃyojanāni
Pahīnāni, pañcudadhambhāgiyāni saṃyojanāni appahīnāni, ito cuttassa tattha uppannassa
kuhiṃ phaluppattī'ti,
Pa. Vi: tattheva.
Anu. ha: hañci anāgāmissa puggalassa pañcorambhāgiyāni saṃyojanāni

tahiṃ phaluppatti.
Anu. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe "natthi devesu brahmacariyavāso"ti.

19. Sa. Pu: anāgāmissa puggalassa pañcorambhāgiyāni saṃyojanāni pahīnāni
Pañcuddhambhāgiyāni saṃyojanāni appahīnāni, ito cutassa tattha
Uppannassa kuhiṃ bhāroharaṇaṃ, kuhiṃ dukkhapariññātaṃ, kuhiṃ
Kilesappahānaṃ, kuhiṃ nirodhasacchikiriyā, kuhiṃ akuppapaṭivedho'ti.
Pa. Vi: tattheva.
Anu. ha. Hañci anāgāmissa puggalassa pañcorambhāgiyani saṃyojanāni
Pahīnāni, pañcuddhambhāgiyāni saṃyojanāni appahīnāni, ito cutassa tattha uppannassa
tahiṃ akuppapaṭivedho.
Anu. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe "natthi devesu brahmacariyavāso"ti.

[A.] Tikaṅguttara.

[BJT Page 268] [\x 268/]

Sa. Pu: anāgāmissa puggalassa pañcorambhāgiyāni saṃyojanāni
Pahīnāni, pañcuddhambhāgiyāti saññojanāni appahīnāni, ito
Cuttassa tattha uppannassa tahiṃ phaluppatti, tihaṃ bhāroharaṇaṃ,

akuppaṭivedho, kenaṭṭhena vadesi

Sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikataṃ, ekadesaṃ sacchikātabbaṃ na
Sacchikatanti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

16. Sa. Pu: maggadassanena kiṃ jahatī'ti.
Pa. Vi: uddhaccaṃ jahati, avijjaṃ tadekaṭṭhe ca kilese jahatī'ti.
Sa. Anu: ekadesaṃ arahā, ekadesaṃ na arahā, ekadesaṃ arahattappatto paṭiladdho adhigato
sacchikato upasampajja
Viharati. (Ekadesaṃ) kāyena phusitvā viharati ekadesaṃ, na kāyena phusitvā viharati.
Ekadesaṃ vītarāgo vītadoso
Vītamoho katakaraṇīyo ohitabhāro anuppattasadattho
Parikkhīṇabhavasaññojano sammadaññāvimutto ukkhittapaligho saṃkiṇṇaparikho
abbūḷhesiko niraggalo ariyo
Pannaddhajo pannabhāro visaññutto suvijitavijayo, dukkhaṃ tassa pariññātaṃ samudayo
pahīno nirodho sacchikato
Maggo bhāvito, abhiññeyyaṃ abhiññātaṃ pariññeyayaṃ
Pariññātaṃ pahātabbaṃ pahīnaṃ bhāvetabbaṃ bhāvitaṃ
Sacchakātabbaṃ sacchikataṃ, (ekadesaṃ sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikataṃ, ) ekadesaṃ
sacchikātabbaṃ na sacchikatanti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

17. Pa. Pu: na vattabbaṃ odhiso'dhiso kilese jahatī'ti.
Sa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.

[BJT Page 288] [\x 288/]

Pa. Anu: nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā:
"Anupubbena medhāvī thoka thokaṃ khaṇe khaṇe
Kammāro rajatasse'va niddhame malamattano'ti. [A]
Attheva suttanto'ti.
Sa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Pa. Niga: tena hi vattabbaṃ. -1. Odhiso'dhiso kilese jahatī"ti.
[PTS Page 109] [\q 109/]

18. Sa. Pu: odhiso'dhiso kilesa jahatī'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā:
Sa. Anu: nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā:
"Sahāvassa dassanasampadāya
Tayassu dhammā jahitā bhavanti:
Sakkāyadiṭṭhi vicikicchitañca
Sīlabbataṃ vā'pi yadatthi kiñci.
Catuhapāyehi ca vippamutto
Cha cābhiṭhānāni abhabbo kātunti" [b.]
Attheva suttanto'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Niga: tena hi na vattabbaṃ "odhiso'dhiso kilese jahatī"ti.

19. Sa. Pu: odhiso'dhiso kilesa jahatī'ti. Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā: "yasmiṃ bhikkhave samaye ariyasāvakassa
Virajaṃ vītamalaṃ dhammacakkhu udapādi: 'yaṃ kiñci samudayadhammaṃ sabbaṃ taṃ
nirodhadhamma'nti. Saha dassanuppādā bhikkhave
Ariyasāvakassa tīṇi saññojanāni pahīyanti: sakkāyadiṭṭhi,
Vicikicchā, sīlabbataparāmāso" ti atthe'va suttanto'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Niga: tena hi na vattabbaṃ odhiso'dhiso kilesa jahatī'ti.

------

1. Ahesuṃ te - sīmu, machasaṃ, [PTS,] syā ahiṃsakā - aṅguttara.
2. Karuṇādhimuttā - sīmu,
Karuṇodhi muttā - machasaṃ, karuṇāvimuttā - [PTS]
3. Kāmasaññojanā - syā, kāmasaññojanāti - [PTS.]
[A.] Aṅguttara chatukkanipāta - dhammikasutta

[BJT Page 302] [\x 302/]

Catunnaṃ dhammānaṃ ananubodhā appaṭivedhā. Katamesaṃ catunnaṃ? Ariyassa sīlassa
ananubodhā appaṭivedhā. Ariyassa samādhissa ariyāya paññāya ariyāya vimuttiyā
ananubodhā appaṭivedhā. Tayidaṃ bhikkhave ariyaṃ sīlaṃ anubuddhaṃ paṭividdhaṃ. Ariyo
samādhi anubuddho paṭividdho. Ariyā paññā anubuddhā paṭividdhā. Ariyā vimutti
anubuddhā paṭividdhā. Ucchinnā bhavatanhā khīṇā bhavanetti. Natthi dāni punabbhavo"ti.

"Sīlaṃ samādhi paññā ca
Vimutti ca anuttarā,
Anubaddhā ime dhammā
Gotamena yasssinā.

Iti buddho abhiññāya
Dhammakkhāsi bhikkhunā, dukkhassantakaro satthā
Cakkhumā parinibbuto"ti. [A.]

Attheva suttanto'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Niga: tena hi na vattabbaṃ "jahati puthujjano kāmarāgyabāpādanti. "

134. Sa. Pu: atītaṃ atthi, anāgataṃ atthi'ti.

Sa. Anu: nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā: "tayo me bhikkhave, niruttipathā
[PTS Page 141] [\q 141/]
Adhivacanapathā paññattipathā asaṅkiṇnā asaṅkiṇṇapubbā na saṅkīyanti na
saṅkīyissanti-1. Appatikuṭṭhā-2. Samaṇehi brāhmaṇehi viññūhi. Katame tayo: yaṃ
bhikkhave rūpaṃ atītaṃniruddhaṃ vigataṃ vipariṇataṃ, 'ahosī'ti tassa saṅkhā, 'ahosī'ti tassa
paññatti. Na tassa saṅkhā 'atthī'ti, na tassa saṅkhā 'bhavissatī'ti. Yā vedanā -pe- yā saññā
-pe- yā saṅkhārā -pe- yaṃ viññāṇaṃ atītaṃ niruddhaṃ vigataṃ vipariṇataṃ, 'ahosī'ti tassa
saṅkhā, 'ahosī'ti tassa samaññā, 'ahosī'ti tassa paññattī. Na tassa saṅkha 'atthi'ti, na tassa
saṅkhā 'bhavissatī'ti.

Yaṃ bhikkhave rūpaṃ ajātaṃ apātubhūtaṃ, 'bhavissatī'ti tassa saṅkhā, 'bhavissatī'ti tassa
samaññā, 'bhavissatī'ti tassa paññatti. Na tassa saṅkhā 'atthi'ti, na tassa saṅkhā 'ahosī'ti. Yā
vedanā -pe- yā saññā -pe- ye saṅkhārā -pe- yaṃ viññāṇaṃ ajātaṃ apātubhūtaṃ, 'bhavissatī'ti
tassa saṅkhā, 'bhavissatī'ti tassa samaññā, 'bhavissatī'ti tassa paññātti. Na tassa
saṅkhā'atthi'ti, na tassa saṅkhā 'ahosī'ti.

1. Na saṅkiyanti na saṅkiyissanti - sīmu, machasaṃ.
2. Appaṭikuṭṭhā - machasaṃ.
Khandha saṃyutta -khandha sutta.

[BJT Page 368] [\x 368/]

Yaṃ bhikkhave rūpaṃ jātaṃ pātubhūtaṃ, 'atthi'ti tassa saṅkhā, 'atthi'ti tassa samaññā, 'atthi'ti
tassa paññatti. Natassa saṅkhā 'ahosī'ti, na tassa saṅkhā 'bhavissatī'ti. Yāvedanā -peyā saññā
-pe- ye saṅkhārā -pe yaṃviññāṇaṃ jātaṃ pātubhūtaṃ, 'atthi'ti tassa saṅkhā, 'atthi'ti tassa
samaññā 'atthi'ti tassa paññatti. Na tassa saṅkhā 'ahosī'ti, na tassa saṅkhā 'bhavissatī'ti.
Ime kho bhikkhavo tayo niruttipathā adhivacanapathā
Paññattipathā asaṅkiṇṇā asaṅkiṇṇapubbā na saṅkiyanti na saṅkīyissanti appatikuṭṭhā
samaṇehi brāhmaṇehi viññūhi. Ye'pi te bhikkhave, ahesuṃ ukkalā vassabhaññā-1.
Ahetukavādā akiriyavādā-2. Natthikavādā, tepi'me tayo niruttipathe adhivacanapathe

viññāṇaṃ virūlhaṃ, atthi [PTS Page 143] [\q 143/]
Tattha nāmarūpassa avakkanti. Yattha atthi nāmarūpassa avakkanti, atthi tattha saṅkhārānaṃ
vuddhi. -3. Yattha atthi saṅkhārānaṃ vuddhi, atthi tattha āyatiṃ punabbhavābhinibbatti.
Yattha atthi āyatiṃ punabbhavābhinibbatti. Yattha atthi āyatiṃ punabbhavābhinibbatti, atthi
tattha āyatiṃ jātijarāmaraṇaṃ. Yattha atthi āyatiṃ jātijarāmaraṇaṃ, sasokaṃ naṃ bhikkhave
sadaraṃ-4. Saupāyāsanti.
------

1. Vattabbaṃ - sīmu.
2. Kabaḷiṃkāre [PTS]
3. Saṅkhārānaṃ buddhi - [PTS]
4. Sarajaṃ - sīmu, machasaṃ, syā. [PTS]ga

Vadāmi. Phasse ce bhikkhave āhāre -pe-
Manosañcetanāya ce bhikkhave āhāre -pe- viññāṇe ce bhikkhave āhāre atthi rāgo, atthi
nandi atthi taṇhā -pesasokaṃ taṃ bhikkhave sadaraṃ saupāyāsanti vadāmī"ti[a.] Attheva
suttantoti.

Sa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Pa. Niga: tena hi anāgataṃ atthiti.
138. Sa. Pu: anāgataṃ atthiti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā: "kabaḷīkāre ce bhikkhave āhāre natthi
Rāgo natthi nandi, natthi taṇhā, appatiṭṭhitaṃ tattha viññāṇaṃ avirūḷhaṃ. Yattha viññāṇaṃ
appatiṭṭhitaṃ avirūḷhaṃ, natthi tattha nāmarūpassa avakkanti. Yattha natthi nāmarūpassa
avakkanti, natthi tattha saṅkhārānaṃ vuddhi. Natthi tattha āyatiṃ punabbhavābhinibbatti.
Yattha natthi āyatiṃ punabbhavā'bhinibbatti, natthi tattha āyatiṃ jātijarāmaraṇaṃ. Yattha
natthi āyatiṃ jātijarāmaraṇaṃ, asokaṃ taṃ bhikkhave ajaraṃ anupāyāsanti vadāmi. Phasse ce
bhikkhave āhāre -pemanosañcatanāya ce bhikkhave āhāre -peviññāṇe ce bhikkhave, āhāre
natthi rāgo, natthi nandi, natthi taṇhā, asokaṃ taṃ bhikkhave ajaraṃ anupāyāsanti
vadāmī"ti[a] attheva suttanto'ti. ?

1. 8.
Ekaccaṃ atthitikathā

1. Sa. Pu: atītaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Vi: ekaccaṃ atthi ekaccaṃ natthi'ti.
Sa. Anu: ekaccaṃ niruddhaṃ, ekaccaṃ na niruddhaṃ, ekaccaṃ vigataṃ,
Ekaccaṃ avigataṃ, ekaccaṃ atthaṅgataṃ, ekaccaṃ na atthaṅgataṃ, ekaccaṃ abbhatthaṅgataṃ,
ekaccaṃ na abbhatthaṅgatanti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

2. Sa. Pu: atītaṃ ekaccaṃ atthi, ekaccaṃ natthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: atītā avipakkavipākā dhammā ekacce atthi, ekacce natthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

3. Sa. Pu: atītaṃ ekaccaṃ atthi, ekaccaṃ natthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: atītā vipakkavipākā dhammā ekacce atthi, ekacce natthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.

Pa. Vi: anāgataṃ anāgatanti hevatthi anāgataṃ atītanti heva natthi, anāgataṃ paccuppannanti
heva natthi'ti.
Sa. Anu: sevatthi seva natthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-
[BJT Page 418] [\x 418/]

10. Sa. Pu: sevatthi seva natthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: atthaṭṭho natthaṭṭho, natthaṭṭho atthaṭṭho, atthibhāvo natthibhāvo, natthibhāvo
atthibhāvo, atthi'ti vā natthi'ti vā, natthi'ti vā atthi'ti vā, esese ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge
tajjāte'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

11. Sa. Pu: paccuppannaṃ hevatthi heva natthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Pu: kintatthi kinti natthi'ti.
[PTS Page 161] [\q 161/]
Pa. Vi: paccuppannaṃ paccuppannanti hevatthi, paccuppannaṃ atītanti
Heva natthi, paccuppannaṃ anāgatanti heva natthi'ti.

Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

12. Sa. Pu: sevatthi seva natthi'ti.

Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

Pa. Anu: atītaṃ anāgatanti hevatthi, atītaṃ paccuppannanti hevatthi, anāgataṃ atītanti
hevatthi, anāgataṃ paccuppannanti hevatthi, paccuppannaṃ atītanti hevatthi, paccuppannaṃ
anāgatanti hevatthi'ti.
Sa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-
Anu. Pā: tena hi atītaṃ hevatthi heva natthi, anāgataṃ hevatthi heva natthi, paccuppannaṃ

-perūpaṃ saṅkhārā'tiheva natthi -pe- rūpaṃ viññāṇanti heva natthi'ti.

Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

19. Sa. Pu: sevatthi seva natthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
[BJT Page 422] [\x 422/]

Sa. Pu: kintatthi kitni natthi'ti.
Pa. Vi: viññāṇaṃ viññāṇanti hevatthi, viññāṇaṃ rūpanti heva natthi -pe- viññāṇaṃ vedanā'ti

Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

[PTS Page 163] [\q 163/]
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

22. Pa. Pu: na vattabbaṃ: "rūpaṃ hevatthi heva natthi'ti, vedanā -pesaññā -pe- saṅkhārā
-tpaviññāṇaṃ hevatthi heva natthi"ti.
Sa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Pa. Anu: rūpaṃ vedanā'ti hevatthi -pe- rūpaṃ saññā'ti hevatthi -pe- rūpaṃ saṅkhārā'ti hevatthi
-perūpaṃ viññāṇanti hevatthi -pe- vedanā -pe- saññā -pe- saṅkhārā -pe viññāṇaṃ rūpanti
hevatthi -pe viññāṇaṃ vedanā'ti hevatthi -pe viññāṇaṃ saññā'ti hevatthi -pe viññāṇaṃ
saṅkhārā'ti hevatthi'ti.
Sa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-
Anu. Pā: tena hi rūpaṃ hevatthi heva natthi, vedanā -pe saññā - saṅkhārā - viññāṇaṃ
hevatthi, heva natthi'ti.
Hevatthikathā niṭṭhitā.
Mahāvaggo.

Tassa uddānaṃ:
Upalabbho parihānaṃ brahmacariyavāso odhiso
Pariññā kāmarāgappahānaṃ sabbatthivādo āyatanaṃ
Atītānāgato subhaṅgo sabbe dhammā satipaṭṭhānā
Hevatthi heva natthi'ti.

1. Sa. Pu: atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhi'ti.

maggo bhāvito, abhiññeyyaṃ abhiññātaṃ pariññeyyaṃ pariññātaṃ [PTS Page 170] [\q 170/]
pahātabbaṃ pahīnaṃ bhāvetabbaṃ bhāvitaṃ sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikatanti.

27. Sa. Pu: atthi arahato aññāṇanti. Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā: "jānato'haṃ-1. Bhikkhave, passato
Āsavānaṃ khayaṃ vadāmi. No ajānato no apassato. Kiñca bhikkhave, jānato kiṃ passato
āsavānaṃ khayo hoti. "Iti rūpaṃ, iti rūpassa samudayo, iti rūpassa atthaṅgamo, iti vedanā -pe-
iti saññā -pe- iti saṅkhārā -pe- iti viññāṇaṃ, iti viññāṇassa samudayo, iti viññāṇassa
atthaṅgamo'ti. Evaṃ kho bhikkhave jānato evaṃ passato āsavānaṃ khayo hotī"ti. [A-] atthe'va
suttanto'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Anu. Pā: tena hi navattabbaṃ: atthi arahato aññāṇanti.

28. Sa. Pu: atthi arahato aññāṇanti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā: "jānato'haṃ-1. Bhikkhave passato
Āsavānaṃ khayaṃ vadāmi. No ajānato no apassato. Kiñca bhikkhave jānato kiṃ passato
āsavānaṃ khayo hoti: idaṃ dukkhanti bhikkhave jānato passato āsavānaṃ khayo hoti. Ayaṃ
dukkhasamudayo'ti jānato passato āsavānaṃ khayo hoti. Ayaṃ dukkhanirodho'ti. Jānato
passato āsavānaṃ khayo hoti. Ayaṃ dukkhanirodhagāminīpaṭipadā'ti jānato pāssato
āsavānaṃ khayo hoti.

Sa.Anu: catubhāgaṃ anāgāmī, catubhāgaṃ na anāgāmī, catubhāgaṃ anāgāmiphalappatto
paṭiladdho adhigato sacchikato upasampajja viharati, kāyena phusitvā viharati, catubhāgaṃ
na kāyena phusitvā viharati, catubhāgaṃ antarāparinibbāyī -pe- upahaccaparinibbāyī
-peasaṅkhāraparinibbāyī -pe- sasaṅkhāraparinibbāyī -peuddhaṃsoto akaṇiṭṭhagāmī,
catubhāgaṃ na uddhaṃsoto akaṇiṭṭhagāmī'ti.

Pa.Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

Vohārakathā

1.Sa.Pu: buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokuttaro'ti.

Pa.Paṭiññā:āmantā.

Sa.Anu: lokuttare sote paṭihaññati no lokiyo, lokuttarena viññānena paṭivijānanti no
lokiyena, sāvakā paṭivijānanti no puthujjanā'ti.

Pa.Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

Anu. ha: hañci buddhassa bhagavato vohāre lokiye sote paṭihaññati,

Anu.Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe: buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokutataro'ti.

Anu.Pā: evamevaṃ bhagavā lokuttarena vohārena lokiyampi lokuttarampi dhammaṃ
voharatī'ti.

17.Sa.Pu: labbhā eḷaṇḍiyāya laṭṭhiyā dhaññapuñjo'pi suvaṇṇapuñjā'pi acikkhitunti.

Pa.Paṭiññā: āmantā.

Anu.Pā: evamevaṃ bhagavā lokiyena vohārena lokiyampi lokuttarampi dhammaṃ
voharati'ti.


18.Sa.Pu: buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokiyaṃ voharantassa lokiyā hoti, lokuttairaṃ
voharantassa lokuttaro hotī'ti.
Pa.Paṭiññā: āmantā.

Sa.Anu: lokiyaṃ voharantassa lokiye sote paṭihaññati, lokuttaraṃ voharantassa lokuttare sote
paṭihaññati, lokiyaṃ voharantassa lokiyena viññāṇena paṭivijānanti, lokuttaraṃ
voharantassa lokuttarena viññāṇena paṭivijānanti, lokiyaṃ voharantassa puthujjanā
paṭivijānanti, lokuttaraṃ voharantassa sāvakā paṭivijānantī'ti.


Pa.Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

19.Pa.Pu: na vattabbaṃ buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokiyaṃ voharantassa lokiyo hoti,
lokuttaraṃ voharantassa lokuttaro hotī'ti.

Sa.Paṭiññā:āmantā.
Pa.Anu: nanu bhagavā lokiyampi lokuttarampi dhammaṃ voharatī'ti.

Sa.Paṭiññā:āmantā.

[BJT Page: 572 [\x 572/] ]

Anu. ha: hañci bhagavā lokiyampi lokuttarampi dhammaṃ voharati,

Anu.Pā: tena vata re vattabbe: buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokiyaṃ voharantassa lokiyo
hoti, lokuttaraṃ voharantassa lokuttaro hotī'ti.

20.Sa.Pu: buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokiyaṃ voharantassa lokiyo hoti, lokuttaraṃ
voharantassa lokuttaro hotī'ti.

Pa.Paṭiññā: āmantā.

Sa.Anu: maggaṃ voharantassa magge hoti, amaggaṃ voharantassa [PTS Page 225] [\q 225/]
amaggo hoti, phalaṃ voharantassa phalaṃ hoti, aphalaṃ voharantassa aphalaṃ hoti,
nibbānaṃ voharantassa nibbānaṃ hoti, anibbānaṃ voharantassa anibbānaṃ hoti, saṅkhataṃ
voharantassa saṅkhataṃ hoti, asaṅkhataṃ voharantassa asaṅkhataṃ hoti, rūpaṃ voharantassa
rūpaṃ hoti, arūpaṃ voharantassa arūpaṃ hoti, vedanaṃ voharantassa vedanā hoti, avedanaṃ
voharantassa avedanā hoti, saññaṃ voharantassa saññā hoti, asaññaṃ voharantassa asaññā
hoti, saṅkhāre voharantassa saṅkhārā honti, asaṅkhāre voharantassa asaṅkhārā honti,
viññāṇaṃ voharantassa viññāṇaṃ hoti, aviññāṇaṃ voharantassa aviññāṇaṃ hotīti.

Pa.Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

Citte parisuddhe pariyodāte anaṅgaṇe
Vigatupakkilese mudubhute kammaniye ṭhite
Āneñajappatte āsavānaṃ khayañāṇāya cittaṃ
Abhininnāmeti"ti[a] attheva suttantoti.

Sa. Paṭi: āmantā.
Anu. Ā: tena hi na vattabbaṃ vimuttaṃ vimuccamānanti.

9. Sa. Pu: atthi cittaṃ vimuccamānanti.
Sa. Paṭi: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: atthi cittaṃ rajjamānaṃ dussamānaṃ vuyhamānaṃ
Kilissamānanti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-
Sa. Anu: nanu rattañceva arattañca duṭṭhañceva
Aduṭṭhañca muḷhañce amuḷhañca dhinnañceva
Acchinnañca bhinnañce abhinnañca katañceva
Akatañcāti.
Sa. Paṭi: āmantā.
Anu. ha: hañci rattañceva arattañca duṭṭhañceva
Aduṭṭhañca muḷhañce amuḷhañca chinnañceva
Acchinnañca bhinnañceva abhinnañca katañceva
Akatañca,
Anu. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe atthi cittaṃ
Vimuccamānanti'.

Anubhāvo gocaroti.

Samannāgatā'ti ca manasi karoti, vacīsucaritena

[BJT Page 134] [\x 134/]
4. 5 Upekkhasamannāgatakathā.
1. Sa. Pu: arahā chahi upekkhāhi samannāgato'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: arahā chahi phassehi chahi vedanāhi chahi saññāhi
-Pe- chahi paññāhi samannāgato'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na vehaṃ vattabbe -pe
2. Sa. Pu: arahā chahi upekkhāhi samannāgato'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: arahā cakkhunā rūpaṃ passanto sotana
Saddaṃ suṇāti, ghanena gandhaṃ ghāyati, jivhāya
Rasaṃ sāyati. Kāyena poṭṭhabbaṃ phusati, manasā
Dhammaṃ vijānāti; manasā dhammaṃ vijānanto
Cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati -pe- sotena saddaṃ
Suṇāti -pe- ghanena gandhaṃ ghāyati -pe-
Jivhāya rasaṃ sāyati -pe- kāyena phoṭṭhabbaṃ phusati'ti.
Pa paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

3. Sa. Pu: arahā chahi upekkhāhi samannāgato'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: sattaṃ samitaṃ abbokiṇṇaṃ1- chahi upekkhāhi
Samannāgato samohito2- cha upekkhāyo
Paccupaṭṭhitā'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-
4. Sa. Pu: na vattabbaṃ arahā chahi upekkhāhi samannāgato'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Pa. Anu: nanu arahā chaḷaṅgupekkho'ti3-
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.

Paṭigaṇhanti1- pacchā manussā'ti.

6. Sa. Pu: yathā bodhisattassa jāyamānassa cattāro naṃ
Devaputtā2- paṭiggahetvā mātu purato ṭhapenti
Attamanā devi3- hohi, mahesakkho tava
Putto uppanno'ti evamevaṃ cakkavatti
Sattassa jāyamānassa cattāro naṃ devaputtā,
Paṭiggahetvā mātu purato ṭhapenti attamanā
Devi hohi mahesakkho tava4- putto uppanno'ti.

Antalikkhā pātubhavanti: ekā sītassa ekā
Uṇhassa, yena bodhisattassa udakakiccaṃ
Karonti mātu ca, evamevaṃ [PTS Page 285] [\q 285/] cakkavattissa
Jāyamānassa dve udakadhārā antalikkhā pātubhavanti:
Ekā sītassa ekā uṇhassa, yena cakkavattisattassa
Udakakiccaṃ karonti mātu cāti.

Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

Sa. Anu: yathā sampatijāto bodhisatto samehi pādehi
Patiṭṭhahitvā uttarena abhimukho sattapadavitihārena6-
Gacchati, sotambhi chatte anudhāriyamāne
Sabbā ca disā viloketi, āsabhiñca vācaṃ
Bhāsati: aggohamasmi lokassa, jeṭṭhohamasmi
Lokassa, soṭṭhohamasmi lokassa, ayamantimājāti,
Natthi dāni punabbhatvā'ti, evamevaṃ sampatijāto
Cakkavattisatto samehi pādehi
Patiṭṭhahitvā uttarena abhimukho sattapadavitihārena
Gacchati, setamhi chatte anudhāriyamāne
Sabbā ca disā viloketi, āsabhiñca vācaṃ bhāsati.
Aggosahasmi -pe- punabbhavo'ti.

Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

-syā, [PTS.]

Obhāsassa mahato bhumicālassa pātubhāvo hotī'ti.

Mahāpurisassa mahāpurisalakkhaṇāti yehi samannāgatassa
[PTS Page 286] [\q 286/] mahāpurisassa dve'va gatiyo bhavanti
Anaññā, sace agāraṃ ajjhāvasati rājā hoti
Cakkavatti dhammiko dhammarājā cāturanto
Vijitāvi janapadatthāvariyappatto sattaratana
Samannāgato. Tassimāni sattaratanāni bhavanti.
Seyyathīdaṃ: cakkaratanaṃ hatthiratanaṃ assaratanaṃ
Maṇiratanaṃ itthiratanaṃ gahapatiratanaṃ parināyaka
Ratanameva sattamaṃ parosahassaṃ kho panassa
Puttā bhavanti surā vīraṅgarūpā parasenappamaddanā.
So imaṃ paṭhaviṃ sāgarapariyantaṃ
Adaṇḍena asatthena dhammena abhivijiya
Ajjhāvasati. Sace kho pana agārasmā anagāriyaṃ
Pabbajati arahaṃ hoti sammāsambuddho loke vivaṭaccado"ti[a] attheva suttanto"ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Anu. Pā: tena hi lakkhaṇasamannāgato bodhisatto'ti.

[A] mahāvaggapāḷi - mahākkhandhaka [b] saccasaṃyutta - dhammaccakkappavattanasutti

4. 10 Saññojanappahāna kathā.
1. Sa. Pu: sabbasaññojanānaṃ pāhānaṃ arahattanti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: arahattamaggena sabbe saññojanā pahiyantī'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

2. Sa. Pu: arahattamaggena sabbe saññojanā pahiyanti'ti
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: arahattamaggena sakkāyadiṭṭhiṃ vicikicchā sīlabbataparāmāsaṃ pajahatīti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

3. Sa. Pu: arahattamaggena sakkāyadiṭṭhiṃ vicikicchā sīlabbataparāmāsaṃ pajahatīti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: nanu tiṇṇaṃ saññojanānaṃ pahānaṃ sotāpattaphalaṃ
Vuttaṃ bhagavatā'ti. Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Anu. ha: hañci tiṇṇaṃ saññojanānaṃ pahānaṃ sotāpattiphalaṃ
Vuttaṃ bhagavatā,
Anu. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe arahattamaggena
Sabbe saññojanā pahiyantī'ti.

4. Sa. Pu: arahattamaggena sabbe saññojanā pahiyanti'ti
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: arahattamaggena oḷārikaṃ kāmarāgaṃ oḷārikaṃ
Vyāpādaṃ pajahatiti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

Anavasesappahānaṃ arahattaṃ vuttaṃ bhagavatā'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Anu: ṭha: hañci rūparāgaarūparāgamānauddhaccaavijjāya
Anavasesappahānaṃ arahattaṃ vuttaṃ bhagavatā,
Anu. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe "arahattamaggena
Sabbe saññojanā pahiyanti"ti.

9. Sa. Pu: na vattabbaṃ sabbe saṃyojanā pahānaṃ arahattanti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Pa. Anu: nanu arahato sabbe saññojanā pahīnā'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā. [PTS Page 300] [\q 300/]
Anu: ṭha: hañci arahato sabbe saññojanā pahīnā,
Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe "sabbasaññojanānaṃ
Pahānaṃ arahatta"nti.
Saññojanappahānakathā niṭṭhitā.
Catuttho vaggo niṭṭhito.

Tassa uddānaṃ:
Gihissa arahā, saha upapattiyā arahā. Arahato
Sabbe dhammā anāsavā. Arahā catūhi phalehi
Samannāgato, evamevaṃ1- jahi upekkhāhi,
Bodhiyā buddho, lakkhaṇa2- samannāgato
Bodhisatto, 3- okkantiniyāmo caritabrahmacariyo,
Paṭipannako phalena samannāgato,
Sabbasaññojanānaṃ pahānaṃ arahattanti.

1. Evameva - [PTS 2.] Salakkhaṇa - sīmu 3. Potthakesu natthi.

[PTS Page 301] [\q 301/]
[BJT Page 184] [\x 184/]

5. 2 Asekhañāṇakathā
1. Sa. Pu: sekhassa asekhañāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: sekho asekhaṃ dhammaṃ jānāti, passati, diṭṭhaṃ
Viditaṃ sacchikataṃ upasampajja viharati, kāyena
Phusitvā viharatī'ti.

Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

Sa. Anu: nanu sekho asekhaṃ dhammaṃ na jānāti,
Na passati, adiṭṭhaṃ aviditaṃ asacchikataṃ
Na usampajja viharati, na kāyena phusitvā viharatī'ti.

Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā

Anu. ha: hañci sekho asekhaṃ dhammaṃ na jānāti,
Na passati, adiṭṭhaṃ aviditaṃ asacchikataṃ
Na upasampajja viharati, na kāyena phusitvā na viharati'ti.


Anu. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe sekhassa asekhaṃ
Ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti. [PTS Page 304] [\q 304/]

2 Sa. Pu: asekhassa asekhaṃ ñāṇaṃ atthi, asekho asekhaṃ dhammaṃ jānāti, passati, viditaṃ
Sacchikataṃ upasampajja viharati, kāyena
Phusitvā viharatī'ti.

Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: sekhassa asekhaṃ ñāṇaṃ atthi, sekho asekhaṃ
Dhammaṃ jānāti, passati, diṭṭhaṃ
Viditaṃ sacchikataṃ upasampajja viharati, kāyena
Phusitvā viharatī'ti.

Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

[BJT Page 192] [\x 192/]
3. Sa. Pu: sekhassa asekhaṃ ñāṇaṃ atthi, sekho asekhaṃ
Dhammaṃ na jānāti, na passati, adiṭṭhaṃ
Aviditaṃ asacchikataṃ na upasampajja viharati, na kāyena
Phusitvā viharatī'ti.

Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: asekhassa asekhaṃ ñāṇaṃ atthi, asekho asekhaṃ
Dhammaṃ na jānāti, na passati, adiṭṭhaṃ
Aviditaṃ asacchikataṃ na upasampajja viharati, na kāyena
Phusitvā viharatī'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

4. Sa. Pu: sekhassa asekha ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: gotrabhuno puggalassa sotāpattimagge ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.

Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

Sa. Anu: sotāpattiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa

Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-
Sa. Anu: sakadāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya -peanāgāmi
Phalasacchikiriyāya -pe- arahattasacchikiriyāya
Paṭipannassa puggalassa arahatte ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

5. Pa. Pu: na vattabbaṃ sekhassa asekhaṃ ñāṇaṃ atthi"ti.
Sa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.

Uḷāro"ti jānāti. "Sāriputto thero, mahā
Moggallāno thero uḷāro"ti jānātī'ti.
Sa. Paññā: āmantā.
Anu. ha: hañci āyasmā anando sekho "bhagavā
Uḷāro"ti jānāti. [PTS Page 305] [\q 305/] "sāriputto thero,
Mahāmoggallāno thero uḷāro"ti jānāti,
Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe sekhassa asekhaṃ
Ṇāṇaṃ atthi'ti.

5. 5 Paṭisambhidākathā
1. Sa. Pu: sabbaṃ ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidā'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: sammutiñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidā'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

2. Sa. Pu: sammutiñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidā'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: ye keci sammutiṃ jānanti, paṭisambhidā pattā'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

3. Sa. Pu: sabbaṃ ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidā'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidā'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-
[PTS Page 310] [\q 310/]
4. Sa. Pu: cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidā'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: ye keci paracittaṃ jānanti, sabbe te paṭisambhidā'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

5. Sa. Pu: sabbaṃ ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidā'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: sabbā paññā paṭisambhidā'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

[BJT Page 210] [\x 210/]
6. Sa. Pu: sabbaṃ paññā paṭisambhidā'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa atthi paññā paṭisambhidā'ti. Pa. Paṭi: na
hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-
Sa. Anu: apokasiṇaṃ -pe- tejokasiṇaṃ -pe-
Vāyokasiṇaṃ -pe- nilakasiṇaṃ -pepitakasiṇaṃ
-Pe- lohitakasiṇaṃ -pe- odātakasiṇaṃ
-Pe- ākāsānañcāyatanaṃ -peviññāṇañcāyatanaṃ
-Pe-ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ -pe-
Nevasaññānāsaññāyatanaṃ samāpannassa -pe-
Dānaṃ dadantassa -pe- cīvaraṃ dadantassa -pe-
Paṇḍapātaṃ dadantassa -pe- senāsanaṃ dadantassa
-Pe- gilānapaccayabhesajjaparikkhāraṃ dadanantassa
Atthi paññā sā paṭisambhidā'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

7. Pa. Su: na vattabbaṃ sabbaṃ ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidā
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Pa. Anu: atthi lokuttarā paññā, sāpaññā na paṭisambhidā'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-
Anu. Pā: tena hi sabbaṃ ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidā'ti.

Paṭisambhidākathā niṭṭhitā.

[BJT Page 212] [\x 212/]
5. 6 Sammutiñāṇakathā.
1. Sa. Pu: na vattabbā: sammutiñāṇaṃ saccārammaṇaññeva
Na aññārammaṇanti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
[PTS Page 311] [\q 311/] pa. Anu: nanu paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa atthi
Ñāṇaṃ, paṭhavikasiṇañca sammutisaccamhi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Anu. ha: hañci paṭhavikasiṇasamāpattiṃ samāpannassa atthi
Ñāṇaṃ paṭhavikasiṇañca sammutisaccamhi,
Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe: sammutiñāṇaṃ
Saccārammaṇaññe'va na aññārammaṇanti.

2. Sa. Pu: na vattabbā: sammutiñāṇaṃ saccārammaṇaññeva
Na aññārammaṇanti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Pa. Anu: nanu āpokasiṇaṃ -pe- tejokasiṇaṃ -pe-
Gilānapaccaya bhesajjaparikkhāraṃ dadantassa atthi
Ñāṇaṃ, gilānapaccaya besajjaparikkhāro ca
Sammutisaccamhi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Anu. ha: hañci gilānapaccayabhesajjaparikkhāraṃ dadantassa
Atthi ñāṇaṃ, gilānapaccayabhesajja parikkhāro ca
Sammutisaccamhi,
Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe: sammutiñāṇaṃ
Saccārammaṇaññe'va na aññārammaṇanti.

3. Sa. Pu: sammutiñāṇaṃ saccārammaṇaññe'va na aññārammaṇanti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Sa. Anu: tena ñāṇena dukkhaṃ parijānāti. Samudayaṃ
Pajahati, nirodhaṃ sacchikaroti, maggaṃ bhāvetī'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

Sammutiñāṇakathā niṭṭhitā.

[BJT Page 214] [\x 214/]
5. 7 Cittārammaṇakathā.
1. Sa. Pu: cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ cittārammaṇaññe'va
Na aññārammaṇanti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Pa. Anu: nanu atthi koci sarāgaṃ cittaṃ sārāgaṃ
Cittanti pajānātī'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Anu. ha: hañci atthi koci sarāgaṃ cittaṃ sarāgaṃ
Cittanti pajānāti,
Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe: cetopariyāye
Ñāṇaṃ cittārammaṇaññe'va na aññārammaṇanti. [PTS Page 312] [\q 312/]
Sa. Anu: nanu atthi koci vitarāgaṃ cittaṃ -pesadosaṃ
Cittaṃ -pe- vitadosaṃ cittaṃ -pesamohaṃ cittaṃ -pevitahohaṃ cittaṃ -pe- saṅkhittaṃ
Cittaṃ -pe- vikkhittaṃ cittaṃ -pe- mahaggataṃ cittaṃ -peamaggahataṃ cittaṃ -pe- sauttaraṃ
cittaṃ -pe- anuttaraṃ cittaṃ -pe- samohiṃ cittaṃ -pe- asamāhitaṃ cittaṃ -pevimuttaṃ cittaṃ
-pe- avimuttaṃ cittaṃ -pe- avimuttaṃ cittaṃnti pajānātī'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Anu. ha: hañci atthi koci avimuttaṃ cittaṃ avimuttaṃ
Cittanti pajānāti,
Anu. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe: cetopariyāye
Ñāṇaṃ cittārammaṇaññe'va na aññārammaṇatti.

2. Sa. Pu: phassārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ vattabbaṃ: cetopariyāye ñāṇanti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Anu. ha: hañci phassārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ vattabbaṃ: cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ,
Anu. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe: cetopariyāye
Ñāṇaṃ cittārammaṇaññe'va aññārammaṇanti.

[BJT Page 216] [\x 216/]
3. Sa. Pu: vedanārammane ñāṇaṃ -pe saññārammaṇe
Ñāṇaṃ - cetanārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ - cittārammaṇe
Ñāṇaṃ - saddhārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ - viriyārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ - sattārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ -
samādhārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ - paññārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ - rāgārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ - dosārammaṇe
ñāṇaṃ - mohārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ - peanottappārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ vattabbaṃ: cotopariyāye
ñāṇanti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā
Anu. ha: hañci anottappārammane ñāṇaṃ vattabbaṃ:
Cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ,
Anu. Pā: no ca vata re vattabbe: cetopariyāye
Ñāṇaṃ cittārammaṇaññe'va na aññārammaṇatti.

4. Sa. Pu: phassārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ vattabbaṃ: cetopariyāye ñāṇanti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: phassapariyayāye ñāṇanti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

5. Sa. Pu: vedanārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ -pe saññārammaṇo
Ñāṇaṃ -pe- anottappārammaṇe ñāṇaṃ na
Vattabbaṃ: cetopariyāye ñāṇanti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu anottappapariyāye ñāṇanti
[PTS Page 313] [\q 313/] pa. Paṭi: na vehaṃ vattabbe -pe-

6. Pa. Pu: na vattabbaṃ: cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ cittārammaṇaññeva
Na aññārammaṇanti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Pa. Anu: nanu cetopariyāye ñāṇa'nti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Anu. ha: hañci cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ,
Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe: cetopariyāye ñāṇaṃ
Cittārammaṇaññe'va na aññārammaṇanti.

Cittārammaṇa kathā niṭṭhitā

[BJT Page 218] [\x 218/]
5. 8 Anāgatañāṇakatha
1. Sa. Pu: anāgate ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: anāgataṃ mulato jānāti, hetuto jānāti,
Nidānato jānāti, sambhavato jānāti, pabhavato
Jānāti, samuṭṭhānato jānāti, āhārato
Jānāti, ārammaṇato jānāti, paccayato
Jānāti, samudayato jānātī'ti.

Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

2. Sa. Pu: anāgate ñāṇaṃ atthiti. Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: anāgataṃ hetupaccayataṃ jānāti, ārammaṇapaccayataṃ
Jānāti, adhipatipaccayataṃ jānāti,
Anantarapaccayataṃ jānāti, samanantarapaccayataṃ jānātī'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

3. Sa. Pu: anāgate ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.

[BJT Page 220] [\x 220/]
Sa. Anu: gotrabhuno puggalassa sotāpattimagge
Ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe
Sa. Anu: sotāpattiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa puggalassa
Sotāpattiphale ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-
Sa. Anu: sakadāgāmī -pe- anāgāmi [PTS Page 314 [\q 314/] -@]paarahattasacchikiriyāya
Paṭipannassa puggalassa arahattena ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

4. Pa. Pu: na vattabbaṃ anāgate ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Pa. Anu: nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā "pāṭalīputtassa kho
Ānanda tayo antarāyā bhavissanti: aggito
Vā udakato vā mithubhedā vā"ti[a] atthe'va
Suttanto"ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Pa. Niga: tena hi anāgate ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.

Anāgatañāṇakathā niṭṭhitā

[A] dīghanikāya - mahāparinibbāna sutta.

[BJT Page 222] [\x 222/]
5. 9 Paccuppannañāṇakathā.
1. Sa. Pu: paccuppanne1- ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: tena ñāṇena taṃ ñāṇaṃ jānātī'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

2. Sa. Pu: tena ñāṇena taṃ jānāti'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: tena ñāṇena taṃ ñāṇaṃ ñāṇanti jānāti'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

3. Sa. Pu: tena ñāṇena taṃ ñāṇaṃ ñāṇanti jānāti'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: taṃ ñāṇaṃ tassa ñāṇassa ārammaṇanti
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

4. Sa. Pu: taṃ ñāṇaṃ ñāṇassa ārammaṇanti
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: tena phassena taṃ phassaṃ phusati, tāya vedanāya
Taṃ vedanaṃ vedati, tāya saññāya taṃ saññaṃ sañjānāti, tāya cetanāya taṃ cetanaṃ
Ceteni, tena cittena taṃ cittaṃ cintoti,
Tena vitakkena taṃ vitakkaṃ vitakketi,
Tena vicārena taṃ vicāraṃ vicāreti. Tāya
Pītiyā taṃ pītiṃ piyāyati, tāya satiyā taṃ
Satiṃ sarati, tāya paññāya taṃ paññaṃ pajānāti,
1. Paṭuppanne - machasaṃ

[BJT Page 224] [\x 224/]
Tena khaggena taṃ khaggaṃ chindati, tena pharasunā [PTS Page 315] [\q 315/] taṃ
pharasuṃ tacchati, tāya kuṭṭārāya taṃ kuṭhāriṃ1- tacchati, tāya vāsiyā taṃ vāsiṃ tacchati,
tāya suciyā taṃ suciṃ sibbeti, tena aṅgulaggena taṃ aṅgulaggaṃ parāmasati, tena nāsikaggena
taṃ nāsikaggaṃ parāmasati, tena matthakena taṃ matthakaṃ parāmasati, tena guthena taṃ
guthaṃ dhovati, tena muttena taṃ muttaṃ dhovati, tena kheḷena taṃ kheḷaṃ dhovati, tena
pubbena taṃ pubbā dhovati, tena lohitena taṃ lohitaṃ dhovatī'ti.

Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

5. Pa. Pu: na vattabbaṃ: paccuppanne ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Pa. Anu: nanu sabbasaṅkhāro aniccato diṭṭhe tampi
Ñāṇaṃ aniccato diṭṭhaṃ hotī'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Anu. ha: hañci sabbasaṅkhāre aniccato diṭṭhe tampi
Ñāṇaṃ aniccato diṭṭhaṃ hoti,
Anu. Pā: tena vata re vattabbe: paccuppanne ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.

Paccuppannañāṇakathā niṭṭhitā.

1. Kudhāriyā taṃ kudhāriṃ - machasaṃ

[BJT Page 226] [\x 226/]
5. 10 Phalañāṇakathā.
1. Sa. Pu: sāvakassa phale ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: sāvako phalassa kataṃ paññāpetī'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

2. Sa. Pu: sāvakassa phale ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: atthi sāvakassa phalaparopariyanti indriyaparopariyanti
Puggalaparopariyantī'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

3. Sa. Pu: sāvakassa phale ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: atthi sāvakassa khandhapaññatti āyatanapaññatti
[PTS Page 316] [\q 316/] dhātupaññatti saccapaññanti indripaññatti
Puggalapaññattī'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

4. Sa. Pu: sāvakassa phale ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: sāvako jino satthā sammāsambuddho sabbaññu
Sabbadassāvī dhammasāmi dhammapaṭisaraṇo'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

5. Sa. Pu: sāvakassa phale ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Sa. Anu: sāvako anuppannassa dhammassa uppādetā
Asañjātassa maggassa sañjanetā anakkhātassa
Maggassa akkhātā maggaññu maggavidu maggakovido'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-

[BJT Page 228] [\x 228/]
6. Pa. Pu: na vattabbaṃ sāvakassa phale ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.
Pa. Paṭiññā: āmantā.
Pa. Anu: sāmako aññāṇi'ti.
Pa. Paṭi: na hevaṃ vattabbe -pe-
Pa. Niga: tena hi sāvakassa phale ñāṇaṃ atthi'ti.

Phalañāṇakathā niṭṭhitā.
Vañcamo vaggo niṭṭhito
Mahāpaṇṇāsako.

Tassa uddānaṃ:
Vimuttiñāṇaṃ vimuttaṃ, 1- sekhassa asekhaṃ2- ñāṇaṃ, viparīte ñāṇaṃ, aniyatassa
niyāmagamanāya atthi ñāṇaṃ, sabbaṃ ñāṇaṃ paṭisambhidā, sammuti ñāṇaṃ, ceto pariyāye
ñāṇaṃ, āgate ñāṇaṃ, paccuppanne ñāṇaṃsāvakaphale ñāṇanti.

1. Vimutti - sīmu 2. Asekhe - sīmu.
